country_event = {
	id = brazil.1
	title = brazil.1.t
	desc = brazil.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_parliament

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = brazil.1"
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
	name = brazil.1.a
		# log = "option:	name = brazil.1.a"
		BRA = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = BRA_anglo_brazilian_research_treaty
				days = 100
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = brazil.1.b
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.1.b"
		add_political_power = 50
		BRA = { country_event = brazil.2 }
	}
}

		AND = {
			has_country_flag = BRA_guyana_war_1857
			tag = BRA

		}
	}

		name = brazil.21.a

		}

			FRA = { clr_country_flag = BRA_guyana_war_1857 }

		}
	}
 }

	country_event = {
		id = brazil.23
		title = brazil.23.t
		desc = brazil.23.d

		is_triggered_only = yes

			name =  brazil.23.a

				add_idea = BRA_Pedro_II
				remove_idea = hos_is_leader
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = BRA_empire_constitutional
			complete_national_focus = BRA_a_deal_with_the_emperor
		}
		option = { #  Empire
			name = brazil.23.b
		# log = "option:			name = brazil.23.b"
			add_political_power = -5
			set_country_flag = brazil_emperor_retired
			swap_ideas = {
				add_idea = BRA_Pedro_II
				remove_idea = hos_is_leader
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				add_idea = parliamentary_monarchy
				remove_idea = constitutional_monarchy
			}
			BRA_Pedro_II={
				remove_country_leader_role = {
				  ideology = conserv
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				Character = BRA_General_Assembly
				Promote_leader = yes
				Country_leader = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					expire = "1947.1.1"
				}
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = BRA_General_Assembly
				Ideology = market_liberal
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrism
				popularity = 0.25
			}
			#remove_ideas = BRA_visconde_de_sinimbu
			set_cosmetic_tag = BRA_empire_constitutional
			complete_national_focus = BRA_power_to_the_commons
		}
	}

 country_event = {
	id = brazil.25
	title = brazil.25.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			BRA = { has_completed_focus = BRA_direct_intervention}
		}
		text = brazil.25.d
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			BRA = { has_completed_focus = BRA_the_second_cisplatine_war }
		}
		text = brazil.25.d_b
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_amazonas

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = brazil.25"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#  Empire historical
	option = {
		name = brazil.25.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.25.a"
		trigger = {
			original_tag = BRA
			NOT = {has_completed_focus = BRA_the_second_cisplatine_war}
		}
		BRA = {
			add_political_power = 35
			load_oob = "BRA_volunteers2"
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = cavalry_equipment
				amount = 1000
				producer = BRA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#Empire traditionalist
		name = brazil.25.a2
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.25.a2"
		trigger = {
			original_tag = BRA
			has_completed_focus = BRA_the_second_cisplatine_war
		}
		add_political_power = 35
		add_manpower = -18000
		NOM = {
			load_oob = "BRA_volunteers"
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = cavalry_equipment
				amount = 1000
				producer = BRA
			}
		}
	}
	##  Uraguay conflict starts
	option = {
		name = brazil.25.b
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.25.b"
		trigger = {
			original_tag = URG
			BRA = { NOT = {has_completed_focus = BRA_the_second_cisplatine_war }}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.5
		remove_ideas = {URG_colorado_blanco_war}
		URC = { ## add BRA desire volunters
			transfer_state = 1097
			transfer_state = 1094
			load_oob = "URC_1857"
			inherit_technology = URG
			inherit_institutions = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = URG
				}
				add_core_of = URC
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = URC
			type = civil_war
		}
		add_civil_war_target = URC
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			original_tag = URG
			BRA = { has_completed_focus = BRA_the_second_cisplatine_war }
		}
		remove_ideas = {URG_colorado_blanco_war}
		URC = {
			transfer_state = 1094
			inherit_technology = URG
			inherit_institutions = yes
			load_oob = "URC_1857-alt"
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = URG
				}
				add_core_of = URC
			}
		}
		NOM = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CIS
			transfer_state = 1097
			inherit_technology = BRA
			inherit_institutions = yes
			set_variable = {pops_primary_culture_array^0 = global.rioplatense}
			load_oob = "CIS_1857"
			1097 = {
				add_core_of = NOM
				remove_core_of = URG
				add_claim_by = URG
			}
			add_state_claim = 300
			add_state_claim = 1081
			add_state_claim = 1094
			add_state_claim = 1096
			hidden_effect = {
				1098={
					remove_core_of = NOM
				}
				set_capital = { state = 300 }
				add_ideas = {
				#POLITICS
				  hos_is_leader
				  no_heir
				  absolute_monarchy

				  #Economic
					civilian_economy
					limited_exports
					two_percent
					normal_taxes
					cl_legal

				  #Population
					stagnation_growth
					border_control
					limited_conscription
					limited_equality
					absolutism

					no_constitution
					no_elections

				  #Culture
					privileged_education
					state_religion

				}
				remove_ideas={
					AFR_history_of_colonial_resistance_1
					AF_T_idea_warrior_might_3
					AF_T_unorganized_tribal_nation_5
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Cisplatine Rebel Council"
					desc = "POLITICS_TEMP_DESC"
					#picture = ""
					expire = 1900.1.1
					ideology = absolutism
					traits = { }
				}
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "David Canabarro"
					#picture = ""
					traits = { }
					skill = 1
					attack_skill = 1
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 1
					logistics_skill = 1
				}

				create_corps_commander = {
				  name = "Antônio de Sousa Netto"
				  #picture = ""
				  traits = { }
				  skill = 1
				  attack_skill = 1
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 1
					logistics_skill = 1
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = URG
						is_owned_by = URC
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = NOM
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					URC = { exists = yes }
					NOT = { has_war_with = URC}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = URC
					type = civil_war
				}
			}
			BRA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = NOM
					modifier = offered_support
				}
			}
		}
		URG = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = URC
				type = civil_war
			}
			add_civil_war_target = URC
			declare_war_on = {
				target = NOM
				type = civil_war
			}
			add_civil_war_target = NOM
		}
	}
	option = { #  everyone else
		name = brazil.25.c
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.25.c"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = URG }
			NOT = { original_tag = BRA }
			NOT = { original_tag = ARG }
		}
	}

	option = { #  Argentinan asstance
		name = brazil.25.d1
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.25.d1"
		trigger = { original_tag = ARG }
		add_manpower = -2000
		URC = { add_manpower = 2000 }
	}
	option = {
		name = brazil.25.d2
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.25.d2"
		trigger = {
			original_tag = ARG
			BRA = { has_completed_focus = BRA_the_second_cisplatine_war }
		}
		ARG = {
			add_manpower = -2000
		}
		URC = {
			add_manpower = 2000
			load_oob = "URC_army_rebels"
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = 1000
				producer = ARG
			}
		}
	}
}

##New United States Minister in Brazil
country_event = {
	id = brazil.foreign.1
	title = brazil.foreign.1.t

	desc = {
		text = brazil.foreign.1.d
		trigger = {
			tag = BRA
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = brazil.foreign.1.d_USA
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
	}

  fire_only_once = yes
  is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = BRA
			#tag = USA
		}
		#year.month.day
		#date > 1861.10.01
		NOT = {
			BRA = { has_war_with = USA }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = brazil.foreign.1.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.foreign.1.a"
		trigger = {
			tag = BRA
		}
		country_event = { id = brazil.foreign.2 days = 1}
		set_country_flag = USA_minister_BRA
    USA = {
      set_country_flag = USA_minister_BRA
    }
	}

	option = {
		name = brazil.foreign.1.b
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.foreign.1.b"
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_minister_BRA
	}
}

##Political consequences of Webb's speech
country_event = {
	id = brazil.foreign.5
	title = brazil.foreign.5.t
	desc = brazil.foreign.5.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger =  {
		tag = BRA
		#date > 1861.10.03
		has_country_flag = USA_minister_BRA
	}
	immediate  = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = brazil.foreign.5"
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = 0.01
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = brazil.foreign.5.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.foreign.5.a"
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = BRA_honor_our_alliance }
			country_event = { id = brazil.foreign.9 days = 149 }
		}
    else_if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = BRA_recognize_csa }
			country_event = { id = brazil.foreign.10 days = 163}
		}
    else_if = {
      limit = {
        tag = BRA
        NOT = { has_completed_focus = BRA_honor_our_alliance }
        NOT = { has_completed_focus = BRA_recognize_csa }
      }
      country_event = { id = brazil.foreign.8 days = 163}
    }
	}
}

#1864.08.10
country_event = {
	id = brazil.foreign.24
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = brazil.foreign.24.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.foreign.24.a"
		trigger = {
			tag = BRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_liberal}
					BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_progressive}
				}
			}
			BRA = {
				complete_national_focus = BRA_direct_intervention
				news_event = { id = brazil.foreign.news.8 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_conservative}
			}
			NOM = {
				transfer_state = 1097
				inherit_technology = URG
				inherit_institutions = yes
				#load_oob = "CIS_1857"
				1097 = {
					add_core_of = NOM
					remove_core_of = URG
					add_claim_by = URG
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = URG
							is_owned_by = URC
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = NOM
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = BRA
					relation = military_access
					active = yes
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = BRA
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = BRA
					relation = guarantee
					active = yes
				}
			}
			URG = {
				if ={
					limit = {
						NOM = { exists = yes }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = NOM
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = NOM
				}
			}
			URC = {
				if ={
					limit = {
						NOM = { exists = yes }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = NOM
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = NOM
				}
			}
			BRA = {
				complete_national_focus = BRA_the_second_cisplatine_war
				news_event = { id = brazil.foreign.news.8 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Amazon
country_event = {
	id = brazil.amazon_colonization.1
	title = brazil.amazon_colonization.t
	desc = {
        text = brazil.amazon_colonization.1.d
		trigger = { tag = BRA }
	}
	desc = {
        text = brazil.amazon_colonization.1.d_USA
		trigger = {	tag = USA }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		#date > 1862.07.11
		OR = {
			tag = BRA
			tag = USA
		}
		BRA = { has_idea = BRA_amazon_colonization }
	}

	option = {
		name = brazil.amazon_colonization.1.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil.amazon_colonization.1.a"
        hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    495 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
                    496 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
                    280 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
                    1323 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
                }
                randomize_temp_variable = {
                    var = africanamericanimmigrants1
                    distribution = uniform
                    min = 10000
                    max = 50000
                }
                set_temp_variable = {
                    africanamericanimmigrants2 = africanamericanimmigrants1
                }
                divide_temp_variable = {
                    africanamericanimmigrants2 = 4
                }
                multiply_temp_variable = { africanamericanimmigrants1 = -1 }
                USA = {
                    add_manpower = var:africanamericanimmigrants1
                }
                495 = {
                    add_manpower = africanamericanimmigrants2
                }
                496 = {
                    add_manpower = africanamericanimmigrants2
                }
                280 = {
                    add_manpower = africanamericanimmigrants2
                }
                1323 = {
                    add_manpower = africanamericanimmigrants2
                }
            }
            BRA = { country_event = { id = brazil.amazon_colonization.1 days = 365 } }
            USA = { country_event = { id = brazil.amazon_colonization.1 days = 365 } }
        }
	}
}

#remove prime-minister
 country_event = {
 	id = brazil_prime_minister.23
 	is_triggered_only = yes
 	hidden = yes
 	option = {
 		name = brazil_prime_minister.23.a
		# log = "option: 		name = brazil_prime_minister.23.a"
 		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister } }
 		if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda }
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_marques_de_olinda
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_abaete}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_visconde_de_abaete
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_sinimbu}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_visconde_de_sinimbu
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_francisco_furtado}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_francisco_furtado
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_barao_de_uruguaiana}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_barao_de_uruguaiana
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_do_rio_branco}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_visconde_do_rio_branco
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_marques_de_paranagua}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_marques_de_paranagua
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_nabuco_de_araujo}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_nabuco_de_araujo
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_duque_de_caxias}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_duque_de_caxias
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_itaborai}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_visconde_de_itaborai
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_conselheiro_saraiva}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_conselheiro_saraiva
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_zacaria_de_gois}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_zacaria_de_gois
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_sao_vicente}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_visconde_de_sao_vicente
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_martinho_campos}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_martinho_campos
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_conselheiro_lafayette}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_conselheiro_lafayette
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_sousa_dantas}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_sousa_dantas
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_barao_de_cotegipe}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_barao_de_cotegipe
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_joao_alfredo}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_joao_alfredo
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_ouro_preto}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_visconde_de_ouro_preto
 		}
 		else_if = {
 			limit = { has_idea = BRA_no_prime_minister}
 			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
 			remove_ideas = BRA_no_prime_minister
 		}
 	}
}

#Add Marquês de Olinda
country_event = {
	id = brazil_prime_minister.1
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = brazil_prime_minister.1.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_prime_minister.1.a"
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_abaete}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_abaete
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_sinimbu}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_sinimbu
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_francisco_furtado}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_francisco_furtado
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_barao_de_uruguaiana}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_barao_de_uruguaiana
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_do_rio_branco}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_do_rio_branco
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_marques_de_paranagua}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_marques_de_paranagua
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_nabuco_de_araujo}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_nabuco_de_araujo
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_duque_de_caxias}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_duque_de_caxias
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_itaborai}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_itaborai
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_conselheiro_saraiva}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_conselheiro_saraiva
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_zacaria_de_gois}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_zacaria_de_gois
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_sao_vicente}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_sao_vicente
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_martinho_campos}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_martinho_campos
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_conselheiro_lafayette}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_conselheiro_lafayette
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = BRA_sousa_dantas}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
				swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_sousa_dantas
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_barao_de_cotegipe}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_barao_de_cotegipe
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_joao_alfredo}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_joao_alfredo
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_ouro_preto}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_ouro_preto
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_no_prime_minister}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_no_prime_minister
				add_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = brazil_prime_minister.2
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = brazil_prime_minister.2.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_prime_minister.2.a"
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
					add_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai
					add_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros

			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_abaete
					add_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros

			}

	id = brazil_prime_minister.3
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = brazil_prime_minister.3.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_prime_minister.3.a"

			limit = { has_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
				add_idea = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai
			}
		}

#Add Francisco Furtado
country_event = {
	id = brazil_prime_minister.6
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = brazil_prime_minister.6.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_prime_minister.6.a"
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
				add_idea = BRA_francisco_furtado
			}
		}
		else_if = {

#Add Conselheiro Saraiva
country_event = {
	id = brazil_prime_minister.13
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = brazil_prime_minister.13.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_prime_minister.13.a"
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
				add_idea = BRA_conselheiro_saraiva
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros
				add_idea = BRA_conselheiro_saraiva
			}
		}
		else_if = {

			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai

#Add Martinho Campos
country_event = {
	id = brazil_prime_minister.16
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = brazil_prime_minister.16.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_prime_minister.16.a"
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda}
			clr_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_marques_de_olinda
				add_idea = BRA_martinho_campos
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros}

				remove_idea = BRA_eusebio_de_queiros

			}
		}
		else_if = {

			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BRA_visconde_de_uruguai

#Ministers Appointed - 1858.12
country_event = {
	id = brazil_prime_minister.appointed.1
	title = brazil_prime_minister.appointed.1.t
	desc =  brazil_prime_minister.appointed.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = brazil_prime_minister.appointed.1"
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = BRA
		date > 1858.12.01
		date < 1858.12.31
 		NOT = { has_idea = BRA_Pedro_II}
	}
	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = brazil_prime_minister.appointed.1"
		set_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
		country_event = { id = brazil_minister_actions.3 }
	}
	option = {#Visconde de Abaeté
		name = brazil_prime_minister.appointed.1.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_prime_minister.appointed.1.a"

			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}

				has_country_flag = brazil_conservative
			}

				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = brazil_liberal

				has_country_flag = brazil_progressive

#EVENTS - BRAZIL ELECTIONS
#COUNTRY EVENTS
add_namespace = brazil_election
#elections alert
country_event = {
	id = brazil_election.18
	title = brazil_election.18.t
	desc = brazil_election.18.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = brazil_election.18"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = BRA_Pedro_II
			}
			set_country_flag = BRA_change_prime_minister
			country_event = { id = brazil_prime_minister.23 days = 20}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1858.12.01
				date<1859.12.01
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.1 days = 20}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1859.12.01
				date<1861.07.01
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.3 days = 20}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1861.07.01
				date<1862.05.01
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.6 days = 20}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1862.05.01
				date<1864.01.01
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.8 days = 20}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1864.01.01
				date<1865.05.01
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.10 days = 20}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1865.05.01
				date<1866.08.01
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.12 days = 20}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1866.08.01
				date<1868.07.01
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.14 days = 20}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1868.07.01
				date<1870.09.01
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.16 days = 20}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = brazil_election.18.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.18.a"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.18 months = 48}
		}
	}
}

#Elections 1858
country_event = {
	id = brazil_election.1
	title = brazil_election.1.t
	desc = brazil_election.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {#abaeté
		name = brazil_election.1.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.1.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 334
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_abaete_1858
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.2 days = 20 }
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.1 days = 27 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
	option = {#queirós
		name = brazil_election.1.b
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.1.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 333
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_queiros_1858
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.2 days = 20 }
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.1 days = 27 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
	option = {#uruguai
		name = brazil_election.1.c
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.1.c"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 333
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_uruguai_1858
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.2 days = 20 }
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.1 days = 27 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
	option = {#sinimbu
		name = brazil_election.1.e
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.1.e"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_sinimbu_1858
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.2 days = 20 }
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.1 days = 27 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = brazil_election.2
	title = brazil_election.2.t
	desc = {
		text = brazil_election.2.d_a
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_abaete_1858 } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = brazil_election.2.d_b
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_queiros_1858 } }

country_event = {
	id = brazil_election.3
	title = brazil_election.3.t
	desc = brazil_election.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = brazil_election.3"
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_abaete_1858 }
					BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_queiros_1858 }
					BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_uruguai_1858 }
					BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_sinimbu_1858 }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = brazil_election.5 hours = 1}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#uruguaiana
		name = brazil_election.3.a
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.3.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 500
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_uruguaiana_1859
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.4 days = 20 }
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.2 days = 27 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
	option = {#riobranco
		name = brazil_election.3.b
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.3.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 500
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_rio_branco_1859
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.4 days = 20 }
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.2 days = 27 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
	option = {#furtado
		name = brazil_election.3.c
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.3.c"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 333
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_furtado_1859
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.4 days = 20 }
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.2 days = 27 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
	option = {#paranagua
		name = brazil_election.3.e
		# log = "option:		name = brazil_election.3.e"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_paranagua_1859
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.4 days = 20 }
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.2 days = 27 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
}

				factor = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = no
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = brazil_martinho_1870
			country_event = { id = brazil_election.17 days = 20}
			news_event = { id = brazil_election.news.8 days = 27}
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.05}
		}
	}
}

	desc = {

		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_sao_vicente_1870 } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = brazil_election.17.d_b
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_martinho_1870 } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {#são vicente
		name = brazil_election.17.a
		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_sao_vicente_1870 } }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "José Antônio Pimenta Bueno"
			desc = ""
			picture = "Portrait_BRA_Pimenta_Bueno.png"
			expire = 1878.02.19
			ideology = conserv
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = traditional_conservatism
		}
	}
	option = {#martinho

		trigger = { BRA = { has_country_flag = brazil_martinho_1870 } }

			name = "Martinho Álvares da Silva Campos"

		}

		}
	}
}

# Hidden event to 'age' Pedro after 1870
country_event = {
	id = brazil.63
	trigger = {
		tag = BRA
		has_country_leader = {
			character = BRA_Pedro_II
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		date > 1870.1.1
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			BRA_Pedro_II = {
				add_corps_commander_role = {
					  skill = 4
					  attack_skill = 2
					  defense_skill = 3
					  planning_skill = 3
					  logistics_skill = 5
					}
				set_leader_portrait = "GFX_Portrait_BRA_Pedro_II"
				remove_unit_leader_role = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = brazil_minister_actions.3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit =  {
				BRA = { has_idea = BRA_Pedro_de_Araujo_Lima_adm }
			}
			deactivate_advisor = BRA_Pedro_de_Araujo_Lima_adm

			#	character = BRA_Pedro_de_Araujo_Lima_adm
			#	slot = political_advisor

		}

			limit =  {
				BRA = { has_idea = BRA_francisco_pereira_jugde }
			}

		}

			limit =  {
				BRA = { has_idea = BRA_viscount_of_maranguape_foreign }
			}

					eoanb_trait_experienced_diplomat
					BRA_trait_foreign_minister
				}
			}
			#activate = yes
		}

			ideology = autocracy
			popularity = -0.01
		}

		}

			character = BRA_marquis_of_muritiba
			advisor = {
				name = "Manuel Vieira Tosta"
				slot = navy_chief

		}

add_namespace = brazil_votes

country_event = { # Brazil Votes 1857_1
	id = brazil_votes.1
	title = brazil_votes.1.t
	desc = brazil_votes.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { # Don't change
			var = current_reform_id
			value = -1									# This allows the system to detect a custom vote in progress
		}
		reset_approval_arrays = yes						# Resets all of the approvals
		#set_1_approval_highly_disagree = yes			# For those ideologies who have a 1 for this type of legislation will highly disagree with this bill
		#set_2_approval_disagree = yes					# For those ideologies who have a 2 for this type of legislation will disagree with this bill
		#set_3_approval_neutral = yes					# For those ideolgoies who have a 3 for this type of legislation will be neutral about this bill
		#set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# For those ideologies who have a 4 for this type of legislation will highly agree with this bill
		set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for planned economy
		set_3_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for autocracy approvals
		set_2_approval_neutral = yes					# Change for conservative approvals
		set_1_approval_neutral = yes					# Change for centrists approvalsroval
		set_vote_eco = yes								# Determines what type of legislation this is, and what values of the ideologies' wishlist will be considered (cul, eco, dem, war, bud)
		compute_voting_approval = yes					# Calculates the approvals
		compute_number_seats_tot = yes					# Calculates the total number of seats in the current Parliament
		compute_number_seats_approve_est = yes			# Estimates the number of seats that will vote yes for the vote
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.1.a
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.1				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 35									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
	option = { # Abandon the idea
		name = brazil_votes.1.b
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}

	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.1.c
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.1				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 1									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
}
country_event = { # Brazil Votes results 1_1857
	id = brazil_votes_results.1
	title = brazil_votes_results.1.t
	desc = brazil_votes_results.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			calculate_vote_result = yes								# Do all the calculations for the vote, and outputs a country flag (eoanb_reform_vote_success, eoanb_reform_vote_failure, eoanb_reform_vote_tie)
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a success!
		name = brazil_votes_results.1.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
			# Put here if the result is a victory
		enact_voted_reform = yes
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
		add_ideas = BRA_medical_school_reform
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = traditional_conservatism }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = centrism }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_liberal }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conciliatory }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_ultraconservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_democracy popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a failure...
		name = brazil_votes_results.1.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
			# Put here if the result is a failure
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a tie.
		name = brazil_votes_results.1.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
			# Put here if the result is a tie
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Brazil Votes results 2_1857
	id = brazil_votes_results.2
	title = brazil_votes_results.2.t
	desc = brazil_votes_results.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			calculate_vote_result = yes								# Do all the calculations for the vote, and outputs a country flag (eoanb_reform_vote_success, eoanb_reform_vote_failure, eoanb_reform_vote_tie)
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a success!
		name = brazil_votes_results.2.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
			# Put here if the result is a victory
		enact_voted_reform = yes
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
		BRA = {
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ENG
				modifier = eoanb_om_ENG_trade_treaty
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = traditional_conservatism }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = centrism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = -0.01 }
		}
				if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_liberal }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}

			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conciliatory }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_ultraconservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_democracy popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a failure...
		name = brazil_votes_results.2.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
			# Put here if the result is a failure
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a tie.
		name = brazil_votes_results.2.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie

country_event = { # Brazil votes results 3_1857
	id = brazil_votes_results.3
	title = brazil_votes_results.3.t
	desc = brazil_votes_results.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			calculate_vote_result = yes								# Do all the calculations for the vote, and outputs a country flag (eoanb_reform_vote_success, eoanb_reform_vote_failure, eoanb_reform_vote_tie)
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a success!
		name = brazil_votes_results.3.a
		trigger = {

		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success

			days = 720
		}

			limit = { has_government = traditional_conservatism }

			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
		}

country_event = { # Brazil Votes 4_1857
	id = brazil_votes.4
	title = brazil_votes.4.t
	desc = brazil_votes.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { # Don't change
			var = current_reform_id
			value = -1									# This allows the system to detect a custom vote in progress
		}
		reset_approval_arrays = yes						# Resets all of the approvals
		set_1_approval_disagree = yes			# For those ideologies who have a 1 for this type of legislation will highly disagree with this bill
		set_2_approval_highly_agree = yes					# For those ideologies who have a 2 for this type of legislation will disagree with this bill
		set_3_approval_highly_agree	= yes					# For those ideolgoies who have a 3 for this type of legislation will be neutral about this bill
		set_4_approval_highly_disagree = yes				# For those ideologies who have a 4 for this type of legislation will highly agree with this bill
		set_vote_eco = yes								# Determines what type of legislation this is, and what values of the ideologies' wishlist will be considered (cul, eco, dem, war, bud)
		compute_voting_approval = yes					# Calculates the approvals
		compute_number_seats_tot = yes					# Calculates the total number of seats in the current Parliament
		compute_number_seats_approve_est = yes			# Estimates the number of seats that will vote yes for the vote
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.4.a
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.4				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 35									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
	option = { # Abandon the idea
		name = brazil_votes.4.b
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}

	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.4.c
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.4				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 1									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
}

			calculate_vote_result = yes								# Do all the calculations for the vote, and outputs a country flag (eoanb_reform_vote_success, eoanb_reform_vote_failure, eoanb_reform_vote_tie)
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a success!
		name = brazil_votes_results.7.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
			# Put here if the result is a victory
		enact_voted_reform = yes
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
		BRA = {
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ENG
				modifier = eoanb_minor_opinion_boost
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = BRA
				modifier = eoanb_minor_opinion_boost
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = traditional_conservatism }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = centrism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_liberal }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conciliatory }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_ultraconservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_democracy popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a failure...
		name = brazil_votes_results.7.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
			# Put here if the result is a failure
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a tie.
		name = brazil_votes_results.7.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
			# Put here if the result is a tie
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

	#increase immigration
country_event = { # Brazil Votes 1857_8
	id = brazil_votes.8
	title = brazil_votes.8.t
	desc = brazil_votes.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { # Don't change
			var = current_reform_id
			value = -1									# This allows the system to detect a custom vote in progress
		}
		reset_approval_arrays = yes						# Resets all of the approvals
		#set_1_approval_highly_disagree = yes			# For those ideologies who have a 1 for this type of legislation will highly disagree with this bill
		#set_2_approval_disagree = yes					# For those ideologies who have a 2 for this type of legislation will disagree with this bill
		#set_3_approval_neutral = yes					# For those ideolgoies who have a 3 for this type of legislation will be neutral about this bill
		#set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# For those ideologies who have a 4 for this type of legislation will highly agree with this bill
		set_1_approval_neutral = yes					# Change for Aristocratic approvals
		set_2_approval_neutral = yes					# Change for Elitist approvals
		set_3_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Favoritist approvals
		set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Egalitarian

		set_vote_dem = yes								# Determines what type of legislation this is, and what values of the ideologies' wishlist will be considered (cul, eco, dem, war, bud)
		compute_voting_approval = yes					# Calculates the approvals
		compute_number_seats_tot = yes					# Calculates the total number of seats in the current Parliament
		compute_number_seats_approve_est = yes			# Estimates the number of seats that will vote yes for the vote
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.8.a
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.8				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 35									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
	option = { # Abandon the idea
		name = brazil_votes.8.b
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.8.c
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.8				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 1									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
}
country_event = { # Brazil Votes results 8_1857
	id = brazil_votes_results.8
	title = brazil_votes_results.8.t
	desc = brazil_votes_results.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			calculate_vote_result = yes								# Do all the calculations for the vote, and outputs a country flag (eoanb_reform_vote_success, eoanb_reform_vote_failure, eoanb_reform_vote_tie)
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a success!
		name = brazil_votes_results.8.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
			# Put here if the result is a victory
		enact_voted_reform = yes
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
		add_ideas = BRA_improve_immigration_act
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = traditional_conservatism }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = centrism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }

			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {

country_event = { # Brazil Votes 1857_12
	id = brazil_votes.12
	title = brazil_votes.12.t
	desc = brazil_votes.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { # Don't change
			var = current_reform_id
			value = -1									# This allows the system to detect a custom vote in progress
		}
		reset_approval_arrays = yes						# Resets all of the approvals
		#set_1_approval_highly_disagree = yes			# For those ideologies who have a 1 for this type of legislation will highly disagree with this bill
		#set_2_approval_disagree = yes					# For those ideologies who have a 2 for this type of legislation will disagree with this bill
		#set_3_approval_neutral = yes					# For those ideolgoies who have a 3 for this type of legislation will be neutral about this bill
		#set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# For those ideologies who have a 4 for this type of legislation will highly agree with this bill
		set_1_approval_highly_agree = yes					# Change for Jingoist approvals
		set_2_approval_highly_agree = yes					# Change for Pro-Militarist approvals
		set_3_approval_disagree = yes						# Change for Anti-Militarist approvals
		set_4_approval_highly_disagree = yes				# Change for Pacifist

		set_vote_war = yes								# Determines what type of legislation this is, and what values of the ideologies' wishlist will be considered (cul, eco, dem, war, bud)
		compute_voting_approval = yes					# Calculates the approvals
		compute_number_seats_tot = yes					# Calculates the total number of seats in the current Parliament
		compute_number_seats_approve_est = yes			# Estimates the number of seats that will vote yes for the vote
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.12.a
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.12				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 35									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
	option = { # Abandon the idea
		name = brazil_votes.12.b
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}

	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.12.c
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.12				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 1									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
}

	id = brazil_votes_results.15
	title = brazil_votes_results.15.t
	desc = brazil_votes_results.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			calculate_vote_result = yes								# Do all the calculations for the vote, and outputs a country flag (eoanb_reform_vote_success, eoanb_reform_vote_failure, eoanb_reform_vote_tie)
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a success!
		name = brazil_votes_results.15.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
			# Put here if the result is a victory
		enact_voted_reform = yes
		# unlock_decision_tooltip = BRA_decision_acquire_gold_from_mines
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = traditional_conservatism }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = centrism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_liberal }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conciliatory }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_ultraconservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_democracy popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a failure...
		name = brazil_votes_results.15.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
			# Put here if the result is a failure
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a tie.
		name = brazil_votes_results.15.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
			# Put here if the result is a tie
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
country_event = { # Brazil Votes 1857_16
	id = brazil_votes.16
	title = brazil_votes.16.t
	desc = brazil_votes.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { # Don't change
			var = current_reform_id
			value = -1									# This allows the system to detect a custom vote in progress
		}
		reset_approval_arrays = yes						# Resets all of the approvals
		#set_1_approval_highly_disagree = yes			# For those ideologies who have a 1 for this type of legislation will highly disagree with this bill
		#set_2_approval_disagree = yes					# For those ideologies who have a 2 for this type of legislation will disagree with this bill
		#set_3_approval_neutral = yes					# For those ideolgoies who have a 3 for this type of legislation will be neutral about this bill
		#set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# For those ideologies who have a 4 for this type of legislation will highly agree with this bill
		set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for planned economy
		set_3_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for autocracy approvals
		set_2_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for conservative approvals
		set_1_approval_highly_disagree = yes					# Change for centrists approvalsroval
		set_vote_eco = yes								# Determines what type of legislation this is, and what values of the ideologies' wishlist will be considered (cul, eco, dem, war, bud)
		compute_voting_approval = yes					# Calculates the approvals
		compute_number_seats_tot = yes					# Calculates the total number of seats in the current Parliament
		compute_number_seats_approve_est = yes			# Estimates the number of seats that will vote yes for the vote
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.16.a
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.16				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 30									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
	option = { # Abandon the idea
		name = brazil_votes.16.b
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}

	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.16.c
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.16				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 1									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Brazil Votes 1857_17
	id = brazil_votes.17
	title = brazil_votes.17.t
	desc = brazil_votes.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { # Don't change
			var = current_reform_id
			value = -1									# This allows the system to detect a custom vote in progress
		}
		reset_approval_arrays = yes						# Resets all of the approvals
		#set_1_approval_highly_disagree = yes			# For those ideologies who have a 1 for this type of legislation will highly disagree with this bill
		#set_2_approval_disagree = yes					# For those ideologies who have a 2 for this type of legislation will disagree with this bill
		#set_3_approval_neutral = yes					# For those ideolgoies who have a 3 for this type of legislation will be neutral about this bill
		#set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# For those ideologies who have a 4 for this type of legislation will highly agree with this bill
		set_1_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Aristocratic approvals
		set_2_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Elitist approvals
		set_3_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Favoritist approvals
		set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Egalitarian

		set_vote_dem = yes								# Determines what type of legislation this is, and what values of the ideologies' wishlist will be considered (cul, eco, dem, war, bud)
		compute_voting_approval = yes					# Calculates the approvals
		compute_number_seats_tot = yes					# Calculates the total number of seats in the current Parliament
		compute_number_seats_approve_est = yes			# Estimates the number of seats that will vote yes for the vote
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.17.a
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.17				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 35									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
	option = { # Abandon the idea
		name = brazil_votes.17.b
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.17.c
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.17				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 1									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Brazil Votes results 19_1857
	id = brazil_votes_results.19
	title = brazil_votes_results.19.t
	desc = brazil_votes_results.19.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			calculate_vote_result = yes								# Do all the calculations for the vote, and outputs a country flag (eoanb_reform_vote_success, eoanb_reform_vote_failure, eoanb_reform_vote_tie)
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a success!
		name = brazil_votes_results.19.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_success
			# Put here if the result is a victory
		enact_voted_reform = yes
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
		add_ideas = BRA_1857_alves_branco_law
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = traditional_conservatism }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = -0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = centrism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_liberal }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_conciliatory }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = traditional_conservatism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = centrism popularity = 0.005 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = brazil_ultraconservative }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_democracy popularity = 0.01 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = autocracy popularity = -0.01 }
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a failure...
		name = brazil_votes_results.19.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_failure
			# Put here if the result is a failure
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
	option = { # It's a tie.
		name = brazil_votes_results.19.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
		}
		clr_country_flag = eoanb_reform_vote_tie
			# Put here if the result is a tie
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
#increase immigration
country_event = { # Brazil Votes 1857_20
	id = brazil_votes.20
	title = brazil_votes.20.t
	desc = brazil_votes.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { # Don't change
			var = current_reform_id
			value = -1									# This allows the system to detect a custom vote in progress
		}
		reset_approval_arrays = yes						# Resets all of the approvals
		#set_1_approval_highly_disagree = yes			# For those ideologies who have a 1 for this type of legislation will highly disagree with this bill
		#set_2_approval_disagree = yes					# For those ideologies who have a 2 for this type of legislation will disagree with this bill
		#set_3_approval_neutral = yes					# For those ideolgoies who have a 3 for this type of legislation will be neutral about this bill
		#set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# For those ideologies who have a 4 for this type of legislation will highly agree with this bill
		set_1_approval_neutral = yes					# Change for Aristocratic approvals
		set_2_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Elitist approvals
		set_3_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Favoritist approvals
		set_4_approval_highly_agree = yes				# Change for Egalitarian

		set_vote_dem = yes								# Determines what type of legislation this is, and what values of the ideologies' wishlist will be considered (cul, eco, dem, war, bud)
		compute_voting_approval = yes					# Calculates the approvals
		compute_number_seats_tot = yes					# Calculates the total number of seats in the current Parliament
		compute_number_seats_approve_est = yes			# Estimates the number of seats that will vote yes for the vote
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.20.a
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.20				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 35									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
	option = { # Abandon the idea
		name = brazil_votes.20.b
		set_variable = {
			var = current_reform_id
			value = 0
		}
	}
	option = { # Let's vote in a month
		name = brazil_votes.20.c
		country_event = {
			id = brazil_votes_results.20				# Sets the custom result event for your custom law
			days = 1									# Usually, a vote takes 30 days. You can go lower, but the timed mission won't be able to show the right amount of time. It's not a big deal because this fires the event by itself, and because the decision does nothing in the case of a custom vote.
		}
	}
}
